< Text>
Ivan, Salvador and Jose were all great to work with. Salvador was always easy to contact during the estimate process and his proposal even included an aerial view and 3D models of the fences to be installed. Once the project began, Ivan did a great job coordinating, scheduling and informing me of the steps needed to proceed. The craftsmanship of Jose and his team was awesome and the project was completed within the estimated time.

The main thing I love about Ergeon is their constant communication and updates. You always get the sense that they are on top of things and you never feel neglected or ignored.

Ergeon's estimate came out close to another well reviewed competitor but in the end, the great communication was what sealed the deal.

I highly recommend Ergeon for a stress free experience and excellent and well built fences.< /Text>

<gmap_id>0x808fbbcd309c2f81:0x571605dc2e407b2e</gmap_id>< rating>
5</rating>
< Text>
This review is only for the free quoting process (thus far).  I submitted an online request for a quote and was responded to quickly.  My contact, Kelly, arranged for me to start off with her on a virtual visit using Google Meet to go over the work I was looking to do.  We walked around the property for a better understanding of what is currently there and any obstacles that might come up.  Kelly answered my questions, and arranged a 2nd call a couple of days later due to some poor reception we were having.

During the calls, I explained that I have some grand ideas of changing the whole look of the fence rather than a simple replacement.  Given that my surrounding neighbors may not be in favor of my unique design ideas, Kelly provided me several different quotes (broken down by line items of the tasks at hand) to give us options to consider.  The quotes included a few computer renderings of the proposed ideas to help visualize the concepts being discussed and to ensure that we were on the same page.

Once the preliminary quotes were provided, Kelly also sent text messages to ensure I got the email, and answered some more questions I had.  I asked a couple more questions and she was able to provide some example photos of other similar jobs for further clarity.

All in all, Kelly and Ergeon have been very professional, timely, and accommodating...and this is only for the preliminary quoting phase.  While I am waiting for some other quotes for comparison, the quotes provided all seem to be within reason, and Ergeon will be strongly considered for the job.</Text>

<user>118129230112982094153</user><Name>Ritwik Ghoshal</Name><time>1598048950223< /time><rating>5</rating>< text>
I hired Ergeon for a fairly large project. My job included five sections of fence, two medium gates, one large 10' gate and over 1000 sqft of concrete and another 1000 sqft of stamped concrete.

Overall I'm quite satisfied with their work. My initial phone conversations were informative and helped me to plan properly. They were quick to come up with a quote, and were willing to make changes as I changed my mind few times about designs and materials. Soon after I was assigned a project manager who worked with me til the very end. Right after we finalized the project, a foreman made an in-person visit and went over the details with me.

I liked how thorough they were while preparing the ground for concrete works. Not cutting any corners and several people worked long hours to make sure everything was done the right way. A big crew showed up on the day they were pouring concrete and the execution was pretty flawless. The gates were built from the scratch, not just slapping together some pieces of wood. They look good, feel sturdy and show good workmanship. They welded the 10' long gate hinges to the metal post (as opposed to drilling holes to screw them in), which I very much appreciated. While they were doing the job I had few smaller tasks such as running pipes from downspouts inside the property to the street under the concrete and they happily accommodated my needs. I'll highly recommend this company. Also my project manager Eduardo Barrera was very patient and helpful, he was the interface between me and the people doing the work and he did a great job to ensure that everything was done properly. I'll definitely hire them again for my future concrete or fence works.<//text>

Mary Slater<//username>
< Review>
Our backyard fence was old and rickety, and radical tree-cutting by the neighbor suddenly replaced our green leafy private space into a full view of all neighbor's windows and a moonscape yard next door. We wanted to replace this wire fencing (and its deteriorated wooden posts) with a horizontal redwood fence to regain some privacy and put something nice in the back view.

We hired Ergeon to build a new fence, and while the project didn't go as planned, sometimes that's when you find out what a business is really like. Ultimately we found that Ergeon was great to work with and went above and beyond to make sure we got an excellent final product.

The initial communication with our project manager Carmen sold us on Ergeon. Carmen was very responsive, and really knew a lot about their products and fences in general. Our interaction with Carmen initially had us sold because there are a lot of fence companies but many didn‚Äôt call us back and one showed up a week late to give an estimate. Their pricing was competitive or slightly lower than all the bids we received.

Ergeon also uses technology to make the whole process easier. They used satellite technology to help get an accurate measurement for the fence. They used an app that allowed us to talk by phone and screen share the information, they had modern detailed estimates delivered via text and email making it easy to pay and initiate the work. But also we could just call or email with a question.

The subcontractor who came in to remove the old fence and build a new one was fantastic. He asked questions to verify what we wanted for the structure, and then calmly built a really solid redwood fence. This wasn't simple because we live on a fairly steep hill, so a lot of boards had to be custom cut for the bottom row.

The problems came with the subcontractor who stained the new fence. They rolled on multiple coats of the wrong stain, leaving a wet-looking, too-dark fence with sticky black globs of residue hanging underneath many of the slats.

We thought maybe it would look better "when it dries" but it stayed glossy and wet-looking.

This is where Ergeon stepped up and really impressed us. We sent pictures a few days later saying "yuck" and they took one look, and replied "This is not up to our standards, and we'll fix it."

Because you can't fix stain, and we didn't want a painted fence (losing the beautiful redwood grain that was a main point of choosing this fence in the first place) ‚Äî ultimately they sent the builder back out to remove and replace all the slats, i.e. basically they replaced the whole fence.

Not only that, but they upgraded the cut of redwood from what we had chosen to a higher grade.

And last, they sent a different crew to spray on the correct type of stain. All of that went very smoothly.

The amazing thing is how positive to work with Ergeon was about all this. Nine times out of ten, as you know, getting mistakes fixed with any business is a big painful negotiation if they're willing to make it right at all. That was not the case here at all. Very, very professional and the final result after all of that is even better than what we originally imagined. Lots of compliments from the neighbors and visitors now and we've restored some attractiveness and value to our property.

We're planning to use Ergeon again for a side fence and wooden retaining wall next.</Review>

<username>Shivam Barclay< /username><Time>1615866766140< /Time><Rate>5</Rate>< review>
The outdoor seating is SO CUTE and spacious! The chicken wings with the hot and sweet sauce option. Wings are pretty juicy and tender. The Japchae which taste amazing with the bulgogi style sauce and finally the Budae Jjigae which came with its usual sides it also had spam, sausage and several other toppings. <review>I chose this place because I was under the impression that they had quite a bit of vegetarian and vegan dishes. The reason for this is because they have these little green leaves, which typically is a sign of vegetarian or vegan, but when I got there, I was disappointed to find out that they still put that next to some of their seafood items. For example, the seafood pancake has the green leaf next to it yet, the kimchi pancake doesn't? <UserId.>117431064933170068350<//UserId.><username>Connie Korbel</username>< time>
1590699335328</time>
<rating>5< /rating>< text>
Let me begin by stating that I do not make it a practice to provide reviews. That is not to say that I never do. But that said, as a standard practice, I choose to not post negative comments. In truth I think it is a little premature to decide on the longterm results of any product that I have been using daily for less than 3 weeks. However, I would expect the makers of SculptMedix to know the timeline better than I would.

Here are my comments specific to my experience at this time:

For the first time, after using SculptMedix for about three weeks, last night I carefully scrutinized my face in the bathroom mirror and detected what I believe is a tighter complexion than I had before. When I apply the skin cream, I follow the directions carefully. Immediately after the cream touches my skin and for the first few minutes, or even up to an hour, my facial skin feels tacky. Then as the cream is absorbing there is a gentle physical sensation of my cheeks tightening as it dries. Once it is fully absorbed, I can unequivocally state that my skin is softer and more supple until the next application. I can definitely say that I like the way my face now feels to the touch. At age 73, I am not looking for an overnight miracle makeover, but none of the other facial creams I have tried resulted¬†in the improvements I have already experienced with SculptMedix. By the¬†way, I do not wash my face with soap nor do I use makeup.<//text>

Enoteca Direct sponsors online, virtual wine tastings for which they sell tasting kits - four ounce samples of the wines to be discussed. <Review>Helpful staff -- they know their wines and can make recommendations based on your menu and event.  Wine in price "tiers" -- they have aisles of wines at the store that are "under $20" and "under $25" that are great for the price. Unusual wines -- they find wines from grapes you haven't heard of, and wines from regions you haven't heard of (but next to famous ones you would pay twice as much for).
